# Software / Tech

**Industry ID:** `software-tech` | **Prefix:** `TECH` | **Target:** 500 bullets

---

### TECH-0001
**Role:** software-engineer | **Theme:** backend-development | **Seniority:** mid | **Verb Context:** systems
**Keywords:** REST API, Node.js, microservices, PostgreSQL, system design

**Scope:** {count} RESTful backend microservices processing {requests}K requests per day
**Result:** reducing average API latency from {before}ms to {after}ms and improving system throughput by {throughput}%

**Variations:**
- **A (Standard):** Developed {count} RESTful backend microservices processing {requests}K requests per day, reducing average API latency from {before}ms to {after}ms and improving system throughput by {throughput}%.
- **B (Result-first):** Reduced API latency from {before}ms to {after}ms by developing {count} backend microservices handling {requests}K daily requests, improving throughput by {throughput}%.
- **C (Impact-led):** Cut API latency from {before}ms to {after}ms and boosted throughput by {throughput}%; built {count} production microservices serving {requests}K requests per day.
- **D (Concise):** Built {count} microservices handling {requests}K daily requests, cut latency from {before}ms to {after}ms, gained {throughput}% throughput.

**Variables:**
  - `{count}`: 3 to 12, step 1 (integer)
  - `{requests}`: 50 to 500, step 50 (integer)
  - `{before}`: 800 to 2000, step 200 (integer)
  - `{after}`: 100 to 400, step 50 (integer)
  - `{throughput}`: 20 to 60, step 5 (percentage)
